[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `lib/mprintf.c` within the `FORMAT_STRING` case, when a non-negative [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprecision [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`prec != [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is specified, the code unconditionally sets  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     len = [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mprec;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     without checking that the target string `str` is at least that long. Later, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe loop  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mfor[0m[1;39m([0m[39m; len && *str; len--[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mOUTCHAR[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*str++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     will happily read beyond the NUL terminator if `prec` exceeds the real length [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof `str`, triggering a wild‐address read.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Location  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Edit `lib/mprintf.c`, around lines [0m[1;36m893[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m897[0m[39m in the `FORMAT_STRING` block.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Strategy  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Replace the existing “prec != [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m” branch  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      else [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39mprec != [0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        len = [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mprec;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      else [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*str == [0m[32m'\0'[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        len = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      else[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        len = [0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      with a bounded‐precision computation that clamps to the real string length:  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      else [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39mprec >= [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Only output up to [0m[32m'prec'[0m[39m bytes and never read past str’s NUL *[0m[35m/[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        size_t max = [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mprec;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        size_t i = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Stride until either NUL or precision limit *[0m[35m/[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mwhile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mi < max && str[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          i++;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        len = i;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      else [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*str == [0m[32m'\0'[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        len = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      else[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        len = [0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Alternatively, if `[0m[1;35mstrnlen[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is available and acceptable in this module, you[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmay replace the loop with:  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      else [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39mprec >= [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        len = [0m[1;35mstrnlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr, [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mprec[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change enforces that `len` never exceeds the actual number of readable [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes in `str`, eliminating the wild read.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It adheres to the standard printf behavior: a precision on `%s` should limit [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutput to at most that many characters, but should never read past the string’s [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mterminator.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All other logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwidth adjustments, padding, quoting[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains untouched, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving existing functionality.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Impact & Side Effects  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Performance**: For strings with precision specified, a small loop [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`strnlen`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is invoked; for the common case of no precision [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`prec == [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, behavior[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis unchanged.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Conformance**: Aligns curl’s internal printf with standard C semantics for [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`%.*s`.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Testing**: Existing printf‐related tests should continue to pass because [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalid uses of precision either specify a smaller or equal bound.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Safety**: No changes to external libraries, harness code, or utility [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctions; patch is localized to `formatf`.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verification  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rebuild curl with AddressSanitizer and repro the fuzzer case to confirm the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrash no longer occurs.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run existing mprintf/printf test suite and protocol tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding dict[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensure no regressions.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m231[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m [0m[1;35mwhile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mresult == CURLE_AGAIN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m232[0m[39m:      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The recurring SEGV in `formatf` is not due to the `%s` length logic in [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`lib/mprintf.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthough guarding against runaway reads is good practice[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Instead, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit stems from calling `[0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, user_start[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand any other `sendf` invocations [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhere a user‐controlled string is passed directly as the `fmt` argument[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `sendf` internally does:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       char *s = [0m[1;35mvaprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfmt, ap[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     so if `fmt` contains any ‘%’ glyphs, `formatf` will consume uninitialized or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout‐of‐bounds varargs, leading to “wild‐addr‐read” crashes. Fuzzer‐supplied data [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcan easily embed ‘%’, triggering this.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Outline[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. In `lib/dict.c`, locate every call to `[0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, X[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` where `X` is derived [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom user input [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. `user_start`, `passwd_start`, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Change each such call into a format‐safe invocation:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, [0m[32m"%s"[0m[39m, X[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      This ensures:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - The format string is a compile‐time literal [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[32m"%s"[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so no spurious `%` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom user data is processed.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `formatf` will read exactly one pointer argument [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`X`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and stop at the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfirst NUL, avoiding wild reads.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Leave calls like `[0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, [0m[32m"CLIENT ..."[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` unchanged, since they already [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muse literal format strings with no embedded `%` that refer to missing args.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `lib/dict.c`.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. In the function `[0m[1;35mdict_do[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m225[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m232[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, change:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        do [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          result = [0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, user_start[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m [0m[1;35mwhile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mresult == CURLE_AGAIN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      into:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        do [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          result = [0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, [0m[32m"%s"[0m[39m, user_start[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m [0m[1;35mwhile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mresult == CURLE_AGAIN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. If there are other places in `dict.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor elsewhere in the `dict` module[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhere user‐controlled buffers are passed directly as `fmt`, apply the identical [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchange:[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, user_buf[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      →  [0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, [0m[32m"%s"[0m[39m, user_buf[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Retain the previous `mprintf.c` patch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe precision‐guard loop[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for extra [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafety, but note that it did not address the root cause. It can remain as is or be [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrolled back; either choice does not reintroduce the crash if the `sendf` changes [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare applied.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Functionality[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Literal, fixed‐string `sendf` calls [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. `[0m[32m"CLIENT ...\r\n"[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are untouched.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - User data is still transmitted verbatim via `[0m[32m"%s"[0m[39m`, preserving semantics.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing tests, harness code, and other callers are unaffected because we only[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madjust calls that misuse format strings.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Why This Works[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By binding the format string to a literal and passing the user buffer as an [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39margument, `formatf` no longer interprets user‐embedded `%` patterns.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The wildcard read in `formatf` is fully eliminated because every `%` that [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mappears in user data is printed harmlessly through the `[0m[32m"%s"[0m[39m` directive.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Side Effects & Mitigation[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If user data contained intentional format sequences [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. `[0m[32m"%02d"[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, they will[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnow be printed verbatim [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlikely the intended behavior for a dictionary client[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No new dependencies or behavior changes outside `lib/dict.c`.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Regression risk is minimal since the original misuse of format strings is [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeing corrected, not altering business logic.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. References[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar safe‐formatting practice is used elsewhere in `curl` when duplicating [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mraw data blocks [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. `[0m[1;35mcurl_easy_setopt[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, [0m[32m"%s"[0m[39m, blob[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The upstream `sendf` documentation implies `fmt` must be a format literal; [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis patch restores that contract.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>lib/dict.[0m[1;92mc:225[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m232[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
